<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тренер.html>тре́нер</a> (5190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тренер.html>тре́нер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tréner</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тренер.html>тре́нера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тренер.html>тре́неры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тренер.html>тре́неров</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тренировавшийся.html>тренирова́вшийся</a> (10578)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***трепать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a> (15109)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">трепати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trepati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*trepati</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">трепа́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trepáty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">трепа́ць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trjepácʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">trépati</i> (first singular <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">trẹ́pljem</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">třepat</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">trepať</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">trzepać</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">třepać</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">tśepaś</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">tśapaś</i>. Further cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">trepsė́ti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stomp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">trapinė́ti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to kick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Prussian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Prussian language">Old Prussian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="prg">ertreppa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to cross</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τραπέω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trapéō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">trepidus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">agitated</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">तृप्र</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tṛprá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unstable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">तृपल</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tṛpala</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unstable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌸𐍂𐌰𐌱𐍉𐌽</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">þrabōn</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to trot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">throb</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trepátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(flax etc)</i> to scutch, to swingle</li>
<li>to pull about, to blow about, to flutter, to tousle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>тре́плет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лихорадка.html>лихора́дка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>tréplet</b> lixorádka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is feverish; he is shivering with fever</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нерв.html>не́рвы</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trepátʹ</b> nérvy komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fray someone's nerves</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языко́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trepátʹ</b> jazykóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) to twaddle; prattle;, blather; chew the fat / rag 2) to blab; blabber</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trepátʹ</b> za vólosy kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pull someone's hair</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear out, to fray, to tear
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:истрепать.html>истрепа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">istrepátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>плечу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trepátʹ</b> kovó-libo po plečú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pat someone's shoulder</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potrepátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to beat up, to maul, to pummel
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potrepátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give a hard life/time
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепать.html>потрепа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potrepátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to mention too often, to make too many references <i>(to)</i>, to hackney
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеться.html>хо́чется</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́во</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne xóčetsja <b>trepátʹ</b> éto vysókoje slóvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I wouldn't like to use this lofty word without a special reason</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:история.html>исто́рии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:имя.html>и́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сталь.html>ста́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вовсю.html>вовсю́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pósle étoj istórii jevó ímja stáli <b>trepátʹ</b> vovsjú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">after that incident, his name became the talk of the town</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:растрепать.html>растрепа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rastrepátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трепаться.html>трепа́ться</a> (10323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trepátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепаться.html>трепа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trepátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">истрепа́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flutter</li>
<li>to get worn out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to twaddle, to prattle, to chew the fat, to chew the rag
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потрепаться.html>потрепа́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">potrepátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blab, to blabber
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:доверять.html>доверя́йте</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:секрет.html>секре́ты</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:потому.html>потому́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>лю́бит</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепаться.html>трепа́ться</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne doverjájte jemú svoí sekréty, potomú što on ljúbit <b>trepátʹsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">don't confide in him because he blabs</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trepátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b>тре<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>па́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 6c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — истрепаться, обтрепаться, натрепаться.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-треп-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепет.html>тре́пет</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trépet</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепет.html>тре́пета</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепет.html>тре́петы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепет.html>тре́петов</a></b>)
</p>

<li>awe, trepidation <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">feeling of fear and reverence</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***трепетать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трепетать.html>трепета́ть</a> (7274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепет.html>тре́пет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trépet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепетать.html>трепета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trepetátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to tremble, to quiver, to flicker
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыло.html>кры́лья</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бабочка.html>ба́бочки</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепетать.html>трепе́щут</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krýlʹja bábočki <b>trepéščut</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the butterfly's wings quiver</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to thrill, to tremble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепетать.html>трепета́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trepetátʹ</b> za kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tremble for someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепетать.html>трепета́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́сли</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trepetátʹ</b> pri mýsli (o)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tremble at the thought (of)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепетать.html>трепета́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trepetátʹ</b> ot rádosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to thrill with delight; be thrilled</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепетать.html>трепета́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ужас.html>у́жаса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trepetátʹ</b> ot úžasa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to shudder/thrill with horror</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fear, to tremble <i>(at)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепетать.html>трепещи́</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trepeščí</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tremble!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепет.html>тре́пет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trépet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепетный.html>тре́петный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trépetnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тре́петнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тре́петней</b>)

<ol><li>trembling, flickering, quivering</li>
<li>anxious

<li>reverent</li>
<li>timid</li>
<li>tender, gentle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трепетный.html>тре́петная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:забота.html>забо́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trépetnaja</b> zabóta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">loving/tender care</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>тре́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:петый.html>пет</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>трепло́</a> (23178)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треп.html>трёп</a>(а́ться)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trep(átʹsja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ло́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ló</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>трепло́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trepló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>трепла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>трёпла</a></i> <i>or</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>треплы́</a></i>, <i>genitive plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>трёпел</a></i> <i>or</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>трепло́в</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> garrulous, mendacious, boastful person, liar</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепать.html>трепа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trepátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ло́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ló</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>трепло́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trepló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>трепла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>трёпла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трепло.html>трёпел</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a tool for beating fibers in the form of three oak planks (the middle of which is an isosceles triangle, and the other two oblique parallelograms), glued together and attached to a lime wedge or handle</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:треп.html>трёп</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ло́</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1*d  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-треп-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смекалка.html>-л</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-о</b>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трескаться.html>тре́скаться</a> (29128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">тре́скать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tréskatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треск.html>треск</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tresk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-atʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The same root appears in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trésnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трещать.html>треща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">treščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снувший</a> (7077)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снувший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trésnuvšij</span>)
</p>

***треснуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снуть</a> (7077)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треск.html>треск</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tresk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trésnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трещать.html>треща́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трескаться.html>тре́скаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crack, to burst, to <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>pop</a>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́ха</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trésnutʹ</b> ot sméxa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to split/burst one's sides (laughing)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рожа.html>ро́жа</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снет</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">a róža ne <b>trésnet</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">are you sure it won't bust your chops?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́сни</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xotʹ <b>trésni</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) no matter what 2) no matter how hard I try;  for the life of me</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:хоть.html>хоть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́сни</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne mogú najtí, xotʹ <b>trésni</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I can't find it for the life of me</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чтоб.html>чтоб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снул</a></b>!, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтоб.html>чтоб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снуть</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">štob ty <b>trésnul</b>!, štob tebé <b>trésnutʹ</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blast you!, damn you!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to (begin to) collapse, to break down</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trésnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquilal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hit <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снуть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голове́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trésnutʹ</b> kovó-libo po golové</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hit/bang smb on the head</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:треть.html>треть</a> (5085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треть.html>треть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tretʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треть.html>тре́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треть.html>тре́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треть.html>трете́й</a></b>)
</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:треть.html>треть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 3-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 8e  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>.
